ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')

          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';

          assert x == y;
          assert x == m;
          assert y == m;
          assert cnt >= 2;
          // contradiction: we are in the else branch where cnt < 2
          assert false;

          assert x == z;
          assert x == m;
          assert z == m;
          assert cnt >= 2;
          assert false;
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          assert y == z;
          assert y == m;
          assert z == m;
          assert cnt >= 2;
          assert false;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert x == a';
          assert y == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == y;
          assert m == x;
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert x == b';
          assert z == b';
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == z;
          assert m == x;
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else {

          assert z == c';

          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == z;
          assert m == y;
          assert cnt >= 2;
        }
      }
    }

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;

    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.

          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {

          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z

ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)

{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';

          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a' by {
            assert a' >= b';
            assert MaxOf(a', b') == a' || MaxOf(a', b') == b';
            assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          }
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a' by {
            assert a' >= c';
            assert MaxOf(a', c') == a' || MaxOf(a', c') == c';
            assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          }
          assert x == a' && y == a' by {
            assert MaxOf(a', b') == x;
            assert MaxOf(a', c') == y;
            assert x == a';
            assert y == a';
          }
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z

          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b' by {
            assert b' >= c';
            assert MaxOf(b', c') == b' || MaxOf(b', c') == c';
            assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';

          assert x == b' && z == b' by {
            assert MaxOf(a', b') == x;
            assert MaxOf(b', c') == z;
            assert x == b';
            assert z == b';

        } else {

  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z

  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  if a > b then a else b

  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')

        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert x == a' && y == a';

          assert m == x;
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert cnt >= 2;

          assert x == b' && z == b';
          assert m == x;

          assert m == y;
          assert cnt >= 2;
        }

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      // We only need to consider positive a', b', c' and the specified maxima.
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        // Determine which variable is the largest.
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // Since x == y == m, cnt >= 2, contradicting cnt == 1
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          // y = MaxOf(a',c') <= b' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = z
          // Both x==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradicting cnt == 1
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        // Show a contradiction by proving that cnt >= 2
        var largest := MaxOf(a', MaxOf(b', c'));
        assert largest == a' || largest == b' || largest == c';
        if largest == a' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b') = a' = x, MaxOf(a',c') = a' = y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if largest == b' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b') = b' = x, MaxOf(b',c') = b' = z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c') = c' = y, MaxOf(b',c') = c' = z
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
        // In each branch, we have two of x,y,z equal to the largest value.
        // Thus the maximum among x,y,z appears at least twice, so cnt >= 2.
        // Therefore cnt cannot be 1, contradiction.
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        // If a' is the largest
        if (a' >= b' && a' >= c') {
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          assert x == y;
        }
        // If b' is the largest
        else if (b' >= a' && b' >= c') {
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          assert x == z;
        }
        // If c' is the largest
        else {
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          assert y == z;
        }
        // In all cases, two of x, y, z are equal, implying cnt >= 2, contradiction
        assert (x == y || x == z || y == z);
        // Since cnt == 1, this leads to a contradiction, so the assumption is impossible
        assert false;
      }

  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 &&
         MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z
      {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c'
        {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          assert x == y;
          assert z <= a';
          assert m == x; // because x==y and z <= x, so max(x,y,z) = x
          assert cnt >= 2; // cnt counts x and y both equal to m
        }
        else if b' >= a' && b' >= c'
        {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          assert x == z;
          assert y <= b';
          assert m == x; // because x==z and y <= x, so max(x,y,z) = x
          assert cnt >= 2; // cnt counts x and z both equal to m
        }
        else
        {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          assert y == z;
          assert x <= c';
          assert m == y; // because y==z and x <= y, so max(x,y,z) = y
          assert cnt >= 2; // cnt counts y and z both equal to m
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
